## Page 8

<span style="font-family:'SourceHanSerifCN-Regular';font-size:10.50pt;color:#333333">授权服务器（Authorization Server）</span><span style="font-family:'SourceHanSerifCN-Regular';font-size:10.50pt;color:#a9a9a9">. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . </span><span style="font-family:'SourceHanSerifCN-Regular';font-size:2.62pt;color:#000000"> </span><span style="font-family:'SourceHanSerifCN-Regular';font-size:10.50pt;color:#333333">295</span>
